    { 1102159003;2;DataItem;                 ;

                               IF BankGrp THEN BEGIN

                                 CurrReport.CREATETOTALS(Amt1,Amt2,DAmnt,CAmnt);

                               GenJnlTemplate.GET("Gen. Journal Batch"."Journal Template Name");

                               IF GenJnlTemplate.Recurring THEN BEGIN
                                 IF GETFILTER("Posting Date") <> '' THEN
                                   AddError(

                                       Text000,

                                 IF GETFILTER("Expiration Date") <> '' THEN
                                   AddError(
                                     STRSUBSTNO(
                                       Text000,
                                       FIELDCAPTION("Expiration Date")));
                                 SETFILTER("Expiration Date",'%1 | %2..',0D,WORKDATE);
                               END;

                                 NoSeries.GET("Gen. Journal Batch"."No. Series");

                               VATEntryCreated := FALSE;

                               CurrReport.CREATETOTALS("Amount (LCY)","Balance (LCY)");


                               docno:="Gen. Journal Line"."Line No.";

                               V_Count:=0;

                                  Section6:=TRUE;
                                  Section7:=TRUE;
                                  Section8:=TRUE;

                                  V_Count+=1;

                                    "Amount (LCY)" := Amount;

                                  AccName := '';
                                  BalAccName := '';
                                  Cust_Vend_Ac :='';
                                  DimValueName :='';
                                  DimValueDescription :='';

                                  DimCode3 :='';
                                  DimName3 :='';
                                  Cust_Vend_AcName :='';
                                  bname :='';
                                  EntityName  :='';


                                  IF NOT EmptyLine THEN BEGIN

                                    AmountError := FALSE;

                                    IF ("Account No." = '') AND ("Bal. Account No." = '') THEN
                                      AddError(STRSUBSTNO(Text001,FIELDCAPTION("Account No."),FIELDCAPTION("Bal. Account No.")))
                                    ELSE
                                      IF ("Account Type" <> "Account Type"::"Fixed Asset") AND
                                         ("Bal. Account Type" <> "Bal. Account Type"::"Fixed Asset")
                                      THEN
                                        TestFixedAssetFields("Gen. Journal Line");
                                    CheckICDocument;
                                    IF "Account No." <> '' THEN
                                      CASE "Account Type" OF
                                        "Account Type"::"G/L Account":
                                          BEGIN
                                            IF ("Gen. Bus. Posting Group" <> '') OR ("Gen. Prod. Posting Group" <> '') OR
                                               ("VAT Bus. Posting Group" <> '') OR ("VAT Prod. Posting Group" <> '')
                                            THEN BEGIN
                                              IF "Gen. Posting Type" = 0 THEN
                                                AddError(STRSUBSTNO(Text002,FIELDCAPTION("Gen. Posting Type")));
                                            END;
                                            IF ("Gen. Posting Type" <> "Gen. Posting Type"::" ") AND
                                               ("VAT Posting" = "VAT Posting"::"Automatic VAT Entry")
                                            THEN BEGIN
                                              IF "VAT Amount" + "VAT Base Amount" <> Amount THEN
                                                AddError(
                                                  STRSUBSTNO(
                                                    Text003,FIELDCAPTION("VAT Amount"),FIELDCAPTION("VAT Base Amount"),
                                                    FIELDCAPTION(Amount)));
                                              IF "Currency Code" <> '' THEN
                                                IF "VAT Amount (LCY)" + "VAT Base Amount (LCY)" <> "Amount (LCY)" THEN
                                                  AddError(
                                                    STRSUBSTNO(
                                                      Text003,FIELDCAPTION("VAT Amount (LCY)"),
                                                      FIELDCAPTION("VAT Base Amount (LCY)"),FIELDCAPTION("Amount (LCY)")));
                                            END;
                                            TestJobFields("Gen. Journal Line");
                                          END;
                                        "Account Type"::Customer,"Account Type"::Vendor:
                                          BEGIN
                                            IF "Gen. Posting Type" <> 0 THEN BEGIN
                                              AddError(
                                                STRSUBSTNO(
                                                  Text004,
                                                  FIELDCAPTION("Gen. Posting Type"),FIELDCAPTION("Account Type"),"Account Type"));
                                            END;
                                            IF ("Gen. Bus. Posting Group" <> '') OR ("Gen. Prod. Posting Group" <> '') OR
                                               ("VAT Bus. Posting Group" <> '') OR ("VAT Prod. Posting Group" <> '')
                                            THEN
                                              AddError(
                                                STRSUBSTNO(
                                                  Text005,
                                                  FIELDCAPTION("Gen. Bus. Posting Group"),FIELDCAPTION("Gen. Prod. Posting Group"),
                                                  FIELDCAPTION("VAT Bus. Posting Group"),FIELDCAPTION("VAT Prod. Posting Group"),
                                                  FIELDCAPTION("Account Type"),"Account Type"));

                                            IF "Document Type" <> 0 THEN BEGIN
                                              IF "Account Type" = "Account Type"::Customer THEN
                                                CASE "Document Type" OF
                                                  "Document Type"::"Credit Memo":
                                                     WarningIfPositiveAmt("Gen. Journal Line");
                                                  "Document Type"::Payment:
                                                     IF ("Applies-to Doc. Type" = "Applies-to Doc. Type"::"Credit Memo") AND
                                                        ("Applies-to Doc. No." <> '')
                                                     THEN
                                                       WarningIfNegativeAmt("Gen. Journal Line")
                                                     ELSE
                                                       WarningIfPositiveAmt("Gen. Journal Line");
                                                  "Document Type"::Refund:
                                                     WarningIfNegativeAmt("Gen. Journal Line");
                                                  ELSE
                                                    WarningIfNegativeAmt("Gen. Journal Line");
                                                END
                                              ELSE
                                                CASE "Document Type" OF
                                                  "Document Type"::"Credit Memo":
                                                     WarningIfNegativeAmt("Gen. Journal Line");
                                                  "Document Type"::Payment:
                                                     IF ("Applies-to Doc. Type" = "Applies-to Doc. Type"::"Credit Memo") AND
                                                        ("Applies-to Doc. No." <> '')
                                                     THEN
                                                       WarningIfPositiveAmt("Gen. Journal Line")
                                                     ELSE
                                                       WarningIfNegativeAmt("Gen. Journal Line");
                                                  "Document Type"::Refund:
                                                     WarningIfPositiveAmt("Gen. Journal Line");
                                                  ELSE
                                                    WarningIfPositiveAmt("Gen. Journal Line");
                                                END
                                            END;

                                            IF Amount * "Sales/Purch. (LCY)" < 0 THEN
                                              AddError(
                                                STRSUBSTNO(

                                            IF "Job No." <> '' THEN
                                              AddError(STRSUBSTNO(Text009,FIELDCAPTION("Job No.")));
                                          END;
                                        "Account Type"::"Bank Account":
                                          BEGIN

                                              AddError(

                                                  Text004,

                                                  FIELDCAPTION("Account Type"),"Account Type"));

                                            IF (Amount < 0) AND ("Bank Payment Type" = "Bank Payment Type"::"Computer Check") THEN
                                              IF NOT "Check Printed" THEN

                                          END;

                                    IF "Bal. Account No." <> '' THEN

                                    IF ("Account No." <> '') AND
                                       NOT "System-Created Entry" AND

                                    //CheckAllocations("Gen. Journal Line");

                                    IF "Posting Date" = 0D THEN
                                      AddError(STRSUBSTNO(Text002,FIELDCAPTION("Posting Date")))
                                    ELSE BEGIN
                                      IF "Posting Date" <> NORMALDATE("Posting Date") THEN
                                        IF ("Account Type" <> "Account Type"::"G/L Account") OR
                                           ("Bal. Account Type" <> "Bal. Account Type"::"G/L Account")
                                        THEN

                                      IF (AllowPostingFrom = 0D) AND (AllowPostingTo = 0D) THEN BEGIN
                                        IF USERID <> '' THEN
                                          IF UserSetup.GET(USERID) THEN BEGIN
                                            AllowPostingFrom := UserSetup."Allow Posting From";
                                            AllowPostingTo := UserSetup."Allow Posting To";
                                          END;
                                        IF (AllowPostingFrom = 0D) AND (AllowPostingTo = 0D) THEN BEGIN
                                          AllowPostingFrom := GLSetup."Allow Posting From";
                                          AllowPostingTo := GLSetup."Allow Posting To";
                                        END;

                                          AllowPostingTo := 12319999D;

                                      IF ("Posting Date" < AllowPostingFrom) OR ("Posting Date" > AllowPostingTo) THEN

                                      END;

                                      AddError(

                                    IF ("Account Type" = "Account Type"::"G/L Account") AND
                                       ("Bal. Account Type" = "Bal. Account Type"::"G/L Account")
                                    THEN
                                      IF "Applies-to Doc. No." <> '' THEN
                                        AddError(STRSUBSTNO(Text009,FIELDCAPTION("Applies-to Doc. No.")));

                                    IF (("Account Type" = "Account Type"::"G/L Account") AND
                                        ("Bal. Account Type" = "Bal. Account Type"::"G/L Account")) OR
                                       ("Document Type" <> "Document Type"::Invoice)
                                    THEN BEGIN
                                      IF PaymentTerms.GET("Payment Terms Code") THEN BEGIN
                                        IF ("Document Type" = "Document Type"::"Credit Memo") AND
                                          (NOT PaymentTerms."Calc. Pmt. Disc. on Cr. Memos")
                                        THEN BEGIN
                                          IF "Pmt. Discount Date" <> 0D THEN
                                            AddError(STRSUBSTNO(Text009,FIELDCAPTION("Pmt. Discount Date")));
                                          IF "Payment Discount %" <> 0 THEN
                                            AddError(STRSUBSTNO(Text018,FIELDCAPTION("Payment Discount %")));
                                        END;
                                      END ELSE BEGIN
                                        IF "Pmt. Discount Date" <> 0D THEN
                                          AddError(STRSUBSTNO(Text009,FIELDCAPTION("Pmt. Discount Date")));
                                        IF "Payment Discount %" <> 0 THEN
                                          AddError(STRSUBSTNO(Text018,FIELDCAPTION("Payment Discount %")));
                                      END;
                                    END;

                                    IF (("Account Type" = "Account Type"::"G/L Account") AND
                                        ("Bal. Account Type" = "Bal. Account Type"::"G/L Account")) OR
                                       ("Applies-to Doc. No." <> '')
                                    THEN
                                      IF "Applies-to ID" <> '' THEN
                                        AddError(STRSUBSTNO(Text009,FIELDCAPTION("Applies-to ID")));

                                    IF ("Account Type" <> "Account Type"::"Bank Account") AND
                                       ("Bal. Account Type" <> "Bal. Account Type"::"Bank Account")
                                    THEN
                                      IF GenJnlLine2."Bank Payment Type" > 0 THEN
                                        AddError(STRSUBSTNO(Text009,FIELDCAPTION("Bank Payment Type")));

                                    IF ("Account No." <> '') AND ("Bal. Account No." <> '') THEN BEGIN
                                      PurchPostingType := FALSE;
                                      SalesPostingType := FALSE;
                                    END;
                                    IF "Account No." <> '' THEN
                                      CASE "Account Type" OF
                                        "Account Type"::"G/L Account":
                                          //CheckGLAcc("Gen. Journal Line",AccName);
                                        //"Account Type"::Customer:
                                          CheckCust("Gen. Journal Line",AccName);
                                        "Account Type"::Vendor:
                                          CheckVend("Gen. Journal Line",AccName);
                                        "Account Type"::"Bank Account":
                                          CheckBankAcc("Gen. Journal Line",AccName);
                                        "Account Type"::"Fixed Asset":
                                          CheckFixedAsset("Gen. Journal Line",AccName);
                                        "Account Type"::"IC Partner":
                                          CheckICPartner("Gen. Journal Line",AccName);
                                      END;
                                    IF "Bal. Account No." <> '' THEN BEGIN
                                      ExchAccGLJnlLine.RUN("Gen. Journal Line");
                                      CASE "Account Type" OF
                                        "Account Type"::"G/L Account":
                                          //CheckGLAcc("Gen. Journal Line",BalAccName);
                                        //"Account Type"::Customer:
                                          CheckCust("Gen. Journal Line",BalAccName);
                                        "Account Type"::Vendor:
                                          CheckVend("Gen. Journal Line",BalAccName);
                                        "Account Type"::"Bank Account":
                                          CheckBankAcc("Gen. Journal Line",BalAccName);
                                        "Account Type"::"Fixed Asset":
                                          CheckFixedAsset("Gen. Journal Line",BalAccName);
                                        "Account Type"::"IC Partner":
                                          CheckICPartner("Gen. Journal Line",AccName);
                                      END;
                                      ExchAccGLJnlLine.RUN("Gen. Journal Line");
                                    END;
                                    {//UPG13R2DEV.begin
                                    JnlLineDim.SETRANGE("Table ID",DATABASE::"Gen. Journal Line");
                                    JnlLineDim.SETRANGE("Journal Template Name","Journal Template Name");
                                    JnlLineDim.SETRANGE("Journal Batch Name","Journal Batch Name");
                                    JnlLineDim.SETRANGE("Journal Line No.","Line No.");
                                    IF NOT DimMgt.CheckJnlLineDimComb(JnlLineDim) THEN
                                      AddError(DimMgt.GetDimCombErr);

                                    TableID[1] := DimMgt.TypeToTableID1("Account Type");
                                    No[1] := "Account No.";
                                    TableID[2] := DimMgt.TypeToTableID1("Bal. Account Type");
                                    No[2] := "Bal. Account No.";
                                    TableID[3] := DATABASE::Job;
                                    No[3] := "Job No.";
                                    TableID[4] := DATABASE::"Salesperson/Purchaser";
                                    No[4] := "Salespers./Purch. Code";
                                    TableID[5] := DATABASE::Campaign;
                                    No[5] := "Campaign No.";
                                    IF NOT DimMgt.CheckJnlLineDimValuePosting(JnlLineDim,TableID,No) THEN
                                      AddError(DimMgt.GetDimValuePostingErr);
                                   }//UPG13R2DEV.end
                                  END;

                                  WHTAmount := 0;

                                  IF "Account Type"="Account Type"::Customer THEN BEGIN
                                    MYGenJnlLine.COPY("Gen. Journal Line");
                                    IF (NOT "Skip WHT") THEN BEGIN
                                      IF WHTPostingSetup.GET(
                                          MYGenJnlLine."WHT Business Posting Group",
                                          MYGenJnlLine."WHT Product Posting Group")
                                      THEN BEGIN
                                        IF (WHTPostingSetup."Realized WHT Type" = WHTPostingSetup."Realized WHT Type"::Payment) THEN
                                          WHTAmount := WHTManagement.ApplyCustCalcWHT(MYGenJnlLine);
                                        IF (WHTPostingSetup."Realized WHT Type" = WHTPostingSetup."Realized WHT Type"::Earliest) THEN
                                          WHTAmount := ABS(WHTManagement.CalcCustExtraWHTForEarliest(MYGenJnlLine));
                                        IF (WHTPostingSetup."Realized WHT Type" = WHTPostingSetup."Realized WHT Type"::Invoice) THEN BEGIN
                                          IF (MYGenJnlLine."WHT Absorb Base" <> 0) THEN
                                            WHTAmount := MYGenJnlLine."WHT Absorb Base" * WHTPostingSetup."WHT %" / 100
                                          ELSE
                                            WHTAmount := MYGenJnlLine.Amount * WHTPostingSetup."WHT %" / 100;
                                        END;
                                      END;
                                      TotalWHTAmount := TotalWHTAmount + WHTAmount;
                                    END;
                                  END ELSE
                                    IF "Account Type"="Account Type"::Vendor THEN BEGIN
                                      MYGenJnlLine.COPY("Gen. Journal Line");
                                      IF (NOT "Skip WHT") THEN BEGIN
                                        IF WHTPostingSetup.GET(
                                          MYGenJnlLine."WHT Business Posting Group",
                                          MYGenJnlLine."WHT Product Posting Group")
                                        THEN BEGIN
                                          IF (WHTPostingSetup."Realized WHT Type" = WHTPostingSetup."Realized WHT Type"::Payment) THEN
                                            WHTAmount := WHTManagement.WHTAmountJournal(MYGenJnlLine,FALSE);
                                          IF (WHTPostingSetup."Realized WHT Type" = WHTPostingSetup."Realized WHT Type"::Earliest) THEN
                                            WHTAmount := ABS(WHTManagement.CalcVendExtraWHTForEarliest(MYGenJnlLine));
                                          IF (WHTPostingSetup."Realized WHT Type" = WHTPostingSetup."Realized WHT Type"::Invoice) THEN BEGIN
                                            IF (MYGenJnlLine."WHT Absorb Base" <> 0) THEN
                                              WHTAmount := ABS(MYGenJnlLine."WHT Absorb Base" * WHTPostingSetup."WHT %" / 100)
                                            ELSE
                                              WHTAmount := ABS(MYGenJnlLine.Amount * WHTPostingSetup."WHT %" / 100);
                                          END;
                                        END;
                                        TotalWHTAmount := TotalWHTAmount + WHTAmount;
                                      END;
                                    END;

                                  CheckBalance;


                                  Mastersetup.GET;
                                  //UPG13R2DEV.begin
                                  IF ("Gen. Journal Line"."Journal Batch Name" = Mastersetup."Gjnl Batch") THEN
                                      BEGIN
                                       User1.SETRANGE(User1."User Name","Gen. Journal Line"."Ref. Batch");
                                         IF User1.FINDFIRST THEN
                                             Uname:=User1."Full Name";
                                      END
                                   ELSE
                                      BEGIN

                                     //UPG13R2DEV.begin
                                       {
                                        User1.SETRANGE(User1."User Name","Gen. Journal Line"."Journal Batch Name");
                                         IF User1.FINDFIRST THEN
                                             Uname:=User1."Full Name";
                                             MESSAGE(FORMAT(Uname));
                                             }



                                  UserName:='YMIDN\'+"Gen. Journal Line"."Journal Batch Name";
                                  User1.SETFILTER("User Name",'=%1',UserName);
                                         IF User1.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
                                             Uname:=User1."Full Name";
                                            // MESSAGE('Ok..'+Format(Uname));
                                             END;

                                  //UPG13R2DEV.end

                                      END;
                                  //UPG13R2DEV.end


                                  {
                                  //yimm
                                  BankAcc.SETRANGE(BankAcc."No.","Gen. Journal Line"."Bal. Account No.");
                                  if BankAcc.findfirst then
                                  BankAccPostingGr.SETRANGE(BankAccPostingGr.Code,BankAcc."Bank Acc. Posting Group");
                                  if BankAccPostingGr.findfirst then
                                  accountno1:=BankAccPostingGr."G/L Bank Account No.";
                                  //message('%1',accountno1);

                                  //GLAccNetChange.SETRANGE(GLAccNetChange."No.",
                                  }

                                  //MESSAGE('%1',"Gen. Journal Line"."Bal. Account No.");


                                  // GenJnl Line Header-section1
                                  MasterSetup1.GET;
                                  IF ( (COMPANYNAME = MasterSetup1."Company Name TBI") OR (COMPANYNAME = MasterSetup1."Company Name YEID")) THEN
                                    BEGIN
                                       ReportHeader.RESET;
                                       IF ReportHeader.GET("Gen. Journal Line"."Journal Template Name",COMPANYNAME) THEN
                                             TextforHeading := ReportHeader."Report Heading";
                                     END
                                  ELSE
                                     TextforHeading := 'TRANSFER SLIP  :';

                                  // GenJnl Line Header-section2
                                  IF "Gen. Journal Line"."Currency Code" <> '' THEN
                                  Section2:=FALSE;

                                  IF "Gen. Journal Line"."Currency Code" = '' THEN
                                  Curr1:='IDR'
                                  ELSE
                                  Curr1:= "Gen. Journal Line"."Currency Code" ;

                                  IF (FCY2LCY=TRUE) THEN
                                  Section2:=FALSE;

                                  // GenJnl Line Header-section3
                                  IF "Gen. Journal Line"."Currency Code" = '' THEN
                                  Section3:=FALSE;

                                  IF (FCY2LCY= TRUE) THEN
                                  Section3:=FALSE;

                                  // GenJnl Line Header-section4
                                  IF (FCY2LCY= FALSE) THEN
                                  Section4:=FALSE;

                                  // GenJnl Line Body-section5
                                  DimValue.RESET;
                                  DimValue.SETRANGE(Code,"Shortcut Dimension 1 Code");
                                  DimValue.SETRANGE(DimValue."Global Dimension No.",1);
                                  IF DimValue.FIND('-') THEN
                                  BEGIN
                                    DimValueName := DimValue.Name;
                                    DimValueDescription := DimValue.Description;
                                  END ELSE
                                  BEGIN
                                    DimValueName := '';
                                    DimValueDescription := '';
                                  END;

                                  //YIMMDEVIP1.0.begin
                                  GLSetup.GET;
                                  DimSetEntry.RESET;
                                  DimSetEntry.SETRANGE(DimSetEntry."Dimension Set ID","Gen. Journal Line"."Dimension Set ID");
                                  DimSetEntry.SETRANGE(DimSetEntry."Dimension Code",GLSetup."Shortcut Dimension 2 Code");
                                  IF DimSetEntry.FINDFIRST THEN
                                     BEGIN
                                        DimCode2:=DimSetEntry."Dimension Value Code";
                                        DimName2:='';
                                        DimValue.RESET;
                                        DimValue.SETRANGE(DimValue."Dimension Code",GLSetup."Shortcut Dimension 2 Code");
                                        DimValue.SETRANGE(Code,DimCode2);
                                        IF DimValue.FIND('-') THEN
                                           BEGIN
                                             DimCode2:=DimValue.Code;
                                             DimName2:=DimValue.Name;
                                           END
                                         ELSE
                                           BEGIN
                                             DimCode2:='';
                                             DimName2:='';
                                           END;
                                     END;

                                  DimSetEntry.SETRANGE(DimSetEntry."Dimension Set ID","Gen. Journal Line"."Dimension Set ID");
                                  DimSetEntry.SETRANGE(DimSetEntry."Dimension Code",GLSetup."Shortcut Dimension 3 Code");
                                  IF DimSetEntry.FINDFIRST THEN
                                     BEGIN
                                        DimCode3:=DimSetEntry."Dimension Value Code";
                                        DimName3:='';
                                        DimValue.RESET;
                                        DimValue.SETRANGE(DimValue."Dimension Code",GLSetup."Shortcut Dimension 3 Code");
                                        DimValue.SETRANGE(Code,DimCode3);
                                        IF DimValue.FIND('-') THEN
                                           BEGIN
                                             DimCode3:=DimValue.Code;
                                             DimName3:=DimValue.Description;
                                           END
                                         ELSE
                                           BEGIN
                                             DimCode3:='';
                                             DimName3:='';
                                           END;
                                     END;


                                  //YIMMDEVIP1.0.end
                                  IF ("Gen. Journal Line"."Currency Code" <> '') THEN
                                   BEGIN
                                    DAmnt:= "Gen. Journal Line"."Debit Amount" / "Gen. Journal Line"."Currency Factor";
                                    CAmnt:= "Gen. Journal Line"."Credit Amount" / "Gen. Journal Line"."Currency Factor";
                                   END
                                  ELSE
                                    BEGIN
                                    DAmnt:=0;
                                    CAmnt:=0;
                                    END;

                                  "Gen. Journal Line"."Ready to Post":=TRUE;
                                  "Gen. Journal Line".MODIFY;


                                  IF ("Gen. Journal Line"."Currency Code" = '') THEN
                                    Section5:=FALSE;

                                  ExchngRate:=1;

                                  IF ("Gen. Journal Line"."Currency Factor" <> 0) THEN
                                   ExchngRate:=ABS(1.0/"Gen. Journal Line"."Currency Factor");

                                  IF (FCY2LCY= TRUE) THEN
                                    Section5:=FALSE;

                                  //OnPostSection
                                  cramount+="Gen. Journal Line"."Credit Amount";
                                  Tot_amt_d_lcy+=ABS(DAmnt);
                                  Tot_amt_c_lcy+=ABS(CAmnt);




                                  //============================ GenJnl Line - Body 6
                                  DimValue.RESET;
                                  DimValue.SETRANGE(Code,"Shortcut Dimension 1 Code");
                                  DimValue.SETRANGE(DimValue."Global Dimension No.",1);
                                  IF DimValue.FIND('-') THEN
                                  BEGIN
                                    DimValueName := DimValue.Name;
                                    DimValueDescription := DimValue.Description;
                                  END ELSE
                                  BEGIN
                                    DimValueName := '';
                                    DimValueDescription := '';
                                  END;

                                  IF ("Gen. Journal Line"."Currency Code" <> '') THEN
                                   BEGIN
                                    DAmnt1:= "Gen. Journal Line"."Debit Amount" / "Gen. Journal Line"."Currency Factor";
                                    CAmnt1:= "Gen. Journal Line"."Credit Amount" / "Gen. Journal Line"."Currency Factor";
                                   END
                                  ELSE
                                    BEGIN
                                    DAmnt1:="Gen. Journal Line"."Debit Amount";
                                    CAmnt1:="Gen. Journal Line"."Credit Amount";
                                    END;

                                  "Gen. Journal Line"."Ready to Post":=TRUE;
                                  "Gen. Journal Line".MODIFY;

                                  {
                                  IF ("Gen. Journal Line"."Currency Code" = '') THEN
                                    CurrReport.SHOWOUTPUT(FALSE);
                                  }

                                  ExchngRate:=1;

                                  IF ("Gen. Journal Line"."Currency Factor" <> 0) THEN
                                   ExchngRate:=ABS(1.0/"Gen. Journal Line"."Currency Factor");


                                  IF (FCY2LCY= FALSE) THEN
                                  Section6:=FALSE;

                                  //==================Body 6 - OnPostSection
                                  cramount+="Gen. Journal Line"."Credit Amount";
                                  Tot_amt_d_lcy1+=ABS(DAmnt1);
                                  Tot_amt_c_lcy1+=ABS(CAmnt1);



                                  //= =====================GenJnl Line Body-section7

                                  //Message('7..');
                                  IF ("Gen. Journal Line"."Currency Code" <> '') THEN
                                   Section7:=FALSE;
                                  "Gen. Journal Line"."Ready to Post":=TRUE;
                                  "Gen. Journal Line".MODIFY;

                                  IF (FCY2LCY=TRUE) THEN
                                   Section7:=FALSE;

                                  DimValue.RESET;
                                  DimValue.SETRANGE(Code,"Shortcut Dimension 1 Code");
                                  DimValue.SETRANGE(DimValue."Global Dimension No.",1);
                                  IF DimValue.FIND('-') THEN
                                  BEGIN
                                    DimValueName := DimValue.Name;
                                    DimValueDescription := DimValue.Description;
                                  END ELSE
                                  BEGIN
                                    DimValueName := '';
                                    DimValueDescription := '';
                                  END;

                                  //YIMMDEVIP1.0.begin
                                  IF ("Gen. Journal Line"."Account Type"="Gen. Journal Line"."Account Type"::Customer) THEN
                                  BEGIN
                                    CustPostSetup.RESET;
                                    CustPostSetup.SETRANGE(CustPostSetup.Code,"Gen. Journal Line"."Posting Group");
                                    IF CustPostSetup.FINDSET THEN
                                      Cust_Vend_Ac := CustPostSetup."Receivables Account";
                                      GLAcc.SETRANGE(GLAcc."No.",Cust_Vend_Ac);
                                      IF GLAcc.FINDFIRST THEN
                                        Cust_Vend_AcName := GLAcc.Name;
                                    Cust.RESET;
                                    Cust.SETRANGE(Cust."No.","Gen. Journal Line"."Account No.");
                                    IF Cust.FINDFIRST THEN
                                      EntityName := Cust.Name;

                                  END ELSE
                                  IF ("Gen. Journal Line"."Account Type"="Gen. Journal Line"."Account Type"::Vendor) THEN
                                  BEGIN
                                    VendPostSetup.RESET;
                                    VendPostSetup.SETRANGE(VendPostSetup.Code,"Gen. Journal Line"."Posting Group");
                                    IF VendPostSetup.FINDFIRST THEN
                                      Cust_Vend_Ac := VendPostSetup."Payables Account";
                                      GLAcc.SETRANGE(GLAcc."No.",Cust_Vend_Ac);
                                      IF GLAcc.FINDFIRST THEN
                                        Cust_Vend_AcName := GLAcc.Name;
                                  END;
                                  //YIMMDEVIP1.0.end


                                  //Neeraj
                                  IF "Gen. Journal Line"."Journal Template Name" = 'PAYMENT' THEN
                                   Desc := "Gen. Journal Line".Description
                                  ELSE
                                   Desc := EntityName;




                                  // ===================== GenJnl Line - Body 8

                                  IF ("Gen. Journal Line"."Bal. Account Type"="Gen. Journal Line"."Bal. Account Type"::"G/L Account") THEN
                                   BEGIN
                                    GLAcc.SETRANGE(GLAcc."No.","Gen. Journal Line"."Bal. Account No.");
                                    IF GLAcc.FINDFIRST THEN
                                    bname := GLAcc.Name;
                                   END ELSE
                                  IF ("Gen. Journal Line"."Bal. Account Type"="Gen. Journal Line"."Bal. Account Type"::"Bank Account") THEN
                                    BEGIN
                                      BankAcc.SETRANGE(BankAcc."No.","Gen. Journal Line"."Bal. Account No.");
                                      IF BankAcc.FINDFIRST THEN
                                       bname:=BankAcc.Name;
                                    END;


                                  IF ("Gen. Journal Line"."Debit Amount" <> 0) THEN BEGIN
                                      Amt1:=0;
                                      Amt2:= "Gen. Journal Line"."Debit Amount";
                                      //Amt2Total := Amt2Total + Amt2; //VK
                                  END;
                                  IF ("Gen. Journal Line"."Credit Amount" <> 0 ) THEN BEGIN
                                     Amt1:="Gen. Journal Line"."Credit Amount";
                                     Amt2:=0;
                                     //Amt1Total := Amt1Total + Amt1; //VK
                                  END;


                                  IF (("Gen. Journal Line"."Bal. Account No." = '') OR ("Gen. Journal Line"."Currency Code"<> ''))THEN
                                    Section8:=FALSE;

                                  IF (FCY2LCY=TRUE) THEN
                                    Section8:=FALSE;

                                  IF BankGrp THEN
                                    Section8:=FALSE;




                                  V_TotalDebitAmt+="Gen. Journal Line"."Debit Amount";
                                  V_TotalCreditAmt+="Gen. Journal Line"."Credit Amount";










                                  //MESSAGE(FORMAT("Gen. Journal Line"."Journal Template Name")+'  '+FORMAT("Gen. Journal Line"."Journal Batch Name")+'  '+format("Line No."));



                                  //MEssage('f  '+format(R_GenJournalLine."Line No.")+'  '+format(R_GenJournalLine."Journal Template Name"));



                                  R_GenJournalLine.RESET;
                                  R_GenJournalLine.SETFILTER(R_GenJournalLine."Journal Template Name",'=%1',"Gen. Journal Line"."Journal Template Name");
                                  R_GenJournalLine.SETFILTER(R_GenJournalLine."Journal Batch Name",'=%1',"Gen. Journal Line"."Journal Batch Name");
                                  R_GenJournalLine.SETFILTER(R_GenJournalLine."Bal. Account No.",'=%1',"Gen. Journal Line"."Bal. Account No.");



                                  //Message(Format(V_GenJournalLine_SlipNoFilter));



                                  IF  V_GenJournalLine_SlipNoFilter<>'' THEN
                                  R_GenJournalLine.SETFILTER(R_GenJournalLine."Slip No.",'=%1',"Gen. Journal Line"."Slip No.");


                                  R_GenJournalLine.SETCURRENTKEY(R_GenJournalLine."Journal Template Name",R_GenJournalLine."Journal Batch Name",R_GenJournalLine."Line No.");



                                  IF R_GenJournalLine.FINDLAST THEN
                                   IF (R_GenJournalLine."Journal Template Name"="Journal Template Name") AND (R_GenJournalLine."Journal Batch Name"="Journal Batch Name") AND (R_GenJournalLine."Line No."="Line No.") THEN
                                    BEGIN



                                            //db
                                         // =================================== GenJnl Line - GroupFooter 9

                                          //UPG13R2DEV.begin


                                        //ActualAmount := Amt1 - Amt2;

                                                  ActualAmount :=  V_TotalCreditAmt - V_TotalDebitAmt;
                                                  V_GrandTotalDebitAmt+=ActualAmount;


                                        //UPG13R2DEV.end





                                        IF (NOT BankGrp) OR (ActualAmount > 0)  THEN
                                        Section9:=FALSE;



                                        IF (ActualAmount = 0)  THEN
                                        Section9:=FALSE;


                                     //   MESSAGE('GF 9..'+FORMAT(Section9));





                                        // ==================================GenJnl Line - GroupFooter 10

                                        //UPG13R2DEV.begin
                                        {

                                        ActualAmount := Amt1 - Amt2;
                                        }

                                        ActualAmount := V_TotalCreditAmt-V_TotalDebitAmt;
                                        //UPG13R2DEV.end



                                        IF (NOT BankGrp) OR (ActualAmount < 0)  THEN
                                        Section10:=FALSE;


                                        IF (ActualAmount = 0)  THEN
                                        Section10:=FALSE;

                                        //Message('%1=%2',ActualAmount,V_GrandTotalDebitAmt);
                                        //db
                                        V_TotalDebitAmt:=0;
                                        V_TotalCreditAmt:=0;


                                  END;





                                  //============================ Footer Code Starts From Here



                                   //db
                                  IF (V_Count=V_GenJournalLines_Count)  THEN
                                   BEGIN
                                        // =================GenJnl Line Footer-section11

                                        IF (("Gen. Journal Line"."Bal. Account No."<> '') OR ("Gen. Journal Line"."Currency Code"<>'')) THEN
                                          Section11:=FALSE;

                                        IF (FCY2LCY=TRUE) THEN
                                          Section11:=FALSE;


                                  //MEssage('11...'+format(Section11));



                                        // ===================GenJnl Line Footer-section12
                                        IF (("Gen. Journal Line"."Bal. Account No."<> '') OR ("Gen. Journal Line"."Currency Code"='')) THEN
                                          Section12:=FALSE;


                                        IF (FCY2LCY=TRUE) THEN
                                          Section12:=FALSE;

                                        // GenJnl Line Footer-section13
                                        IF (FCY2LCY=FALSE) THEN
                                          Section13:=FALSE;

                                        // GenJnl Line Footer-section14
                                        ActualAmountLCY := DAmnt - CAmnt;

                                        IF (("Gen. Journal Line"."Bal. Account No." = '') OR ("Gen. Journal Line"."Currency Code" = '')
                                             OR (ActualAmountLCY > 0) OR ("Gen. Journal Line".Amount > 0 ) )THEN
                                          Section14:=FALSE;

                                        GLAcc.SETRANGE(GLAcc."No.","Gen. Journal Line"."Bal. Account No.");
                                        IF GLAcc.FINDFIRST THEN
                                        bname := GLAcc.Name;

                                        IF (FCY2LCY=TRUE) THEN
                                          Section14:=FALSE;

                                        // GenJnl Line Footer-section15
                                        ActualAmountLCY := DAmnt - CAmnt;

                                        IF (("Gen. Journal Line"."Bal. Account No." = '') OR ("Gen. Journal Line"."Currency Code" = '')
                                             OR (ActualAmountLCY > 0) OR ("Gen. Journal Line".Amount < 0 ))THEN
                                          Section15:=FALSE;

                                        GLAcc.SETRANGE(GLAcc."No.","Gen. Journal Line"."Bal. Account No.");
                                        IF GLAcc.FINDFIRST THEN
                                        bname := GLAcc.Name;

                                        IF (FCY2LCY=TRUE) THEN
                                          Section15:=FALSE;

                                        // GenJnl Line Footer-section16
                                        ActualAmountLCY := DAmnt - CAmnt;

                                        IF (("Gen. Journal Line"."Bal. Account No." = '') OR ("Gen. Journal Line"."Currency Code" = '')
                                             OR (ActualAmountLCY < 0))THEN
                                          Section16:=FALSE;

                                        GLAcc.SETRANGE(GLAcc."No.","Gen. Journal Line"."Bal. Account No.");
                                        IF GLAcc.FINDFIRST THEN
                                        bname := GLAcc.Name;

                                        IF (FCY2LCY=TRUE) THEN
                                          Section16:=FALSE;

                                        // GenJnl Line Body-section17
                                        IF (("Gen. Journal Line"."Bal. Account No." = '') OR ("Gen. Journal Line"."Currency Code"<> ''))THEN
                                          Section17:=FALSE;

                                        IF ("Gen. Journal Line"."Bal. Account Type"="Gen. Journal Line"."Bal. Account Type"::"G/L Account") THEN
                                         BEGIN
                                          GLAcc.SETRANGE(GLAcc."No.","Gen. Journal Line"."Bal. Account No.");
                                          IF GLAcc.FINDFIRST THEN
                                          bname := GLAcc.Name;
                                         END ELSE
                                        IF ("Gen. Journal Line"."Bal. Account Type"="Gen. Journal Line"."Bal. Account Type"::"Bank Account") THEN
                                          BEGIN

                                            IF BankAcc.FINDFIRST THEN
                                             bname:=BankAcc.Name;
                                           END;

                                        IF (FCY2LCY=TRUE) THEN
                                          Section17:=FALSE;

                                        IF BankGrp THEN
                                          Section17:=FALSE;

                                          Section18:=FALSE;

                                        IF (ActualAmount >= 0)  THEN
                                          Section18:=FALSE;


                                  //'      MESSAGE(FORMAT(Section18)+'  '+FORMAT(ActualAmount));

                                        IF (NOT BankGrp)THEN
                                          Section19:=FALSE;

                                        IF (ActualAmount <= 0)  THEN
                                          Section19:=FALSE;


                                  END;

                                  IF BnameNew = '' THEN
                                  BnameNew += "Gen. Journal Line"."Bank Name Cust/Vend";
                                  IF BnoNew = '' THEN
                                  BnoNew += "Gen. Journal Line"."Bank Account No.";
                                  IF BeneName = '' THEN
                                  BeneName += "Gen. Journal Line"."Bank Branch No.";
                                END;

               DataItemLinkReference=Gen. Journal Batch;

                            Journal Batch Name=FIELD(Name) }
